## FAQ

<details>
<summary><strong>How often is this list updated?</strong></summary>

Once a day. A GitHub Action pulls new internship postings from Dreamwork's public API, which crawls company career pages directly (Greenhouse, Lever, Ashby, Workday, and others). Use <kbd>Ctrl</kbd>+<kbd>F</kbd> for software engineering, data science, ML, product, or design roles.

</details>

<details>
<summary><strong>Which season are these internships for?</strong></summary>

Whatever companies are hiring for right now. In 2026 that is primarily Fall 2026, Spring 2027, and Summer 2027. New season postings appear here the day Dreamwork first verifies them.

</details>

<details>
<summary><strong>Why are some internships missing?</strong></summary>

This board is intentionally limited to verified-open US tech internships with an internship or co-op title. Closed, duplicate, non-US, and non-tech roles are removed automatically.

</details>

<details>
<summary><strong>Graduating soon?</strong></summary>

The companion list, <a href="https://github.com/dreamworkhq/New-Grad-Software-Engineer-Jobs">New Grad Software Engineer Jobs</a>, covers entry-level full-time roles with the same daily refresh.

</details>

<details>
<summary><strong>Can Dreamwork match these roles to my resume?</strong></summary>

Yes. <a href="https://www.dreamworkhq.com/?utm_source=github&utm_medium=faq&utm_campaign=gh-tech-internships">Dreamwork</a> ranks every role against your resume, goals, seniority, and location. Seeing your matches is free.

</details>

## How this list is built

A [GitHub Action](.github/workflows/update.yml) runs once a day. It queries Dreamwork's public listings API, filters for 2026–2027 tech internships (software engineering, data science, security, product, design) in the United States, removes duplicates, and rewrites this README. The raw snapshot lives in [`data/listings.json`](data/listings.json). Listings are crawled directly from company career pages and ATS boards (Greenhouse, Lever, Ashby, Workday, and others), so links go to real, currently open postings. Found a bad listing? [Open an issue](../../issues).
